Dear All,

I attach a paper to appear in the AI Magazine, Special Issue on Ontologies,
probably in November 2002. In this paper, I have tried to give a comprehensive
overview of the methodology we have applied to the CIDOC CRM, and to motivate
what I'd like to call a "property-centric ontology". I hope this will be helpful for
our discussion. Comments, criticism, most welcome.

best wishes,

Martin
